 In 1984 and 1989 also this seat remained with the National Conference and Abdul Rashik Kabuli and Mohammed Safi Bhat became MP respectively
 1996 main yah seat congress ke khate main chali gai or gulam mohammad mir maagaamee jite
 In 1998, 1999 and 2004, this seat again came to the National Conference and three times Omar Abdullah became MP
 iske baad 2009 main is seat se faruk abdulla utre or jite, lekin 2014 kaa chunaav vah haar gaye
 He was defeated by Tariq Hamid Karra of PDP
 iske baad 2017 main hue upachunaav main ek baar phir faruk abdulla is seat se saansad bane
 The Social Tanabanashrinagar Lok Sabha seat consists of 15 assembly seats (kangan, Ganderbal, Hazratbal, Jadibal, Idgah, Khanyar, Habakdal, Amirkadal, Sonwar, Batmaloo, Chandura, Budgam, Veerwah, Khansahib and charar-e-sharif)
 2014 ke vidhansabha chunaav main is loksabhaa seat kii in 15 siton par neshnal conference or pidipi ke bich kadi takkar hui thi
 The National Conference has 7 seats (kangan, Ganderbal, Idgah, Khanyar, Habakdal, Budgam, Veerwah) and PDP has 8 (hazratbal, Jadibal, Amirkadal, Sonwar, Batmaloo, Chadura, Khansahib, charar-e-sharif) seats
 is seat par 12 lakh 05 hajaar registerd matadaata hai
 There are 6 lakh 30 thousand male and 5 lakh 74 thousand female voters
 2014 kaa janadesh2017 ke upachunaav main neshnal conference ke faruk abdulla 10,776 voton se jite the
